1b1(rgyug): rgya gar skad du
2a1(rgyud): badz+ra kI la ya mu la tan khan rA/ bod skad du/ 
2a2(rgyud): rdo rje phur pa rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi dum bu/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu la phyag
2a3(rgyud): 'tshal lo// rdo rje khro bos zhes snang gcod// mtshon chen sngon po mer 'bar ga/ 
2b1(rgyud): nam mkha'i dkyil du thig le shar// srog gi sgo ru shar ba dang / snying gi dkyil du bsgom par bya/ snying rjes
2b2(rgyud): bsgral ba'i dam tshig ni// gsad cing glanan pa nyid yin te/ pur ba rdo rje'i de nyid de/ rnam par shes pa rdo rjer bsgom// 
2b3(rgyud): oM badz+ra ki le ki lA ya sarba big+h+nAn bam snru ba / dista tsa kA ha na ha na hUM phakra/ rdo rje gzhon nu'i rigs 'dzin rnams// 'khon
2b4(rgyud): ba rdo rjer sgrub par mdzod// 'khor ba rdo rjer phur pa'i lha// ye shes khro bo grub par mdzod// sangs rgyas kun gyi ye shes sku/ 
2b5(rgyud): rdo rje'i de nyid rang bzhin las/ chos kyi dbyings kyi ngo bo nyid// 'bar ba'i khro bo mi bzad pasku'i gter du bdag
3a1(rgyud): skyed cig/ thabs kyi spyod pas sems can don// byams dang snying rjes gang 'dul ba// sangs rgyas
3a2(rgyud): 'phrin las rdzogs par mdzad// dbang dang byin brlabs 'dir rtsol cig// oM badz+ra krod+had+hu kA ra/ ShAn+tu/  ga rna nub
3a3(rgyud): oM badz+ra kro d+ha di pa ya ti hUM/ oM badz+ra u sau ka mu~M kha n+tu/ oM badz+ra u shi ka mu khA n+tu// 'di ni khro bo chen po hUM mdzad dang / 
3a4(rgyud): rdo rje lha mo sgra 'byin dang / sbrul gyi lha mo 'bru man ma phrag gi mgo nan dung/ rnangs pa'i mgo can dang / oM bad+d+ha kr-i d+hA
3a5(rgyud): rgyun na na / rlu /  skye sa ni byA Sh+TA s+'u byu bI d+hA r+m+ma rgyu/ 'dzim
3b1(rgyud): chen po rnam par rgyal ba dang / lha mo sgeg mo dang / sprul pa'i 'phra men ma stag gis mgo con dang / bya rgod kyi mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha ni la da
3b2(rgyud): hUM phaT/ oM badz+ra kro d+hi tA tA ru hUM/ oM badz+ra tsa ma ra mu kha ts+tsha/ oM badz+ra tAka mu kha hUMkaMSh+T+r-i'adi ni khro bo dbyug sngon 'chang ba dang / lha mo rdo rjes sder mo dang
3b3(rgyud): s+phul pa'i lha mo ga yag mgo can dang / k+Shi bya rog gI mgo can no// au yA man ta badz+ra kro d+ha hUM pa tsa pa tsa hUM/ au badz+ra kro d+hista na pa ti hUM/ au ba
3b4(rgyud): hA ri Na mu kha hUM/ oM badz+ra u lu ka mu kha hUM/ 'di ni khro bo ga shin rje mthar byed dang / lha mo dur khrod kyi bdag mo dang / sprul pa'i lha mo
3b5(rgyud): 'bra men ma ri dgas kyi mgo can dang / 'ug pa'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha ar+ya a tsa la hUM/ b+han d+ha b+han d+ha hUM phaT/ !au badz+ra kro d+hi mu ha
3b6(rgyud): oM badz+ra r+yaM gi mu khA hU~M/ oM badz+ra pre ta mu kha hUM/ 'di ni khro bo mi g.yo mgon po dang / rdo rje lha mo gtun khung ma dang / sprul pa
4a1(rgyud): lha mo 'bru men ma gzig gi mgo can dang / khwa'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha ha yaM g+ni ba hu lu hu lu hUM phaT/ oM badz+ra kro ta dza ya ti hUM/ 
4a2(rgyud): oM badz+ra kro d+ha bi ra la mu khA hUM/ oM badz+ra pa k+Shi ta mu khi hUM/ 'di ni khro bo rta mgrin dang / rdo rje lha mo gtun mo dang / sprul pa'i lha mo 'phra men ma byi la'i mgo
4a3(rgyud): tsun dang / phu ba ba shud kyi mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha a pa rA dzi ta hUM/  tiSh+Tha tiSh+Tha hUM phaT/ oM badz+ra krod d+ha se bya ti hUM/ oM badz+ra s+thi ga la mu khyA hUM/ oM badz+ra sany+tsa ra mu khyA
4a4(rgyud): 'di ni khro bo gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang / rdo rje lha mo mnga' snyems ma dang / sprul pa'i lha mo 'phra men ma spyang khu'i mgo can dang / khra'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra
4a5(rgyud): kro d+ha a mi tA kun d+ha li hU~M/ rgyun d+hA tshin d+ha dz+nyA phaT/ oM badz+rA k+Sho d+his bya sa ti hU~M/ oM badz+ra si ha mu kha hU~M// oM badz+ra tid+d+hi la mu kha hUM/ 'di ni khro bo bdud rtsi laH
4a6(rgyud): pa dang / rdo rje lha mo sgra mdzad ma dang / sprul pa'i lha mo 'phra men ma seng ge'i mgo can dang / pa wang gi mA go can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha tAM log kyi badz+ra ya hUM/  b+hin d+ha b+hin
4b1(rgyud): hUM phaT/ oM badz+ra kro d+ha mi rA ya hUM// oM badz+ra ri kA sa mu kha hUM/ oM badz+ra na ku la mu kha hUM/ 'di ni khro bo 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba dang // rdo rje lha mo gsod byed ma dang / sprul
4b2(rgyud): pa'i lha mo 'bru min ma rnyed kyi mgo can dpe sre mo'i mgo can no// oM badz+ra kro d+ha ma hA bA la hUM s+pho Ta s+phoT hUM phana~M/ oM badz+ra kro d+hi mudz+dzi ma hU~M/ oM badz+ra ra k+Sha sa mu kha hUM/ oM badz+ra ki shi ka mu
4b3(rgyud): khyahUM/ 'di ni khro bo stobs po che dang / rdo rje lha mo rigs byed ma dpa' sprul pa'i lha mo 'bru man ma dang / dom gyi mgo can dang // byi ba'i mgo n+dan no// / oM bar+d+ha yak+Sha s+yA da ts+tsha dza/ oM byAd+d+ha
4b4(rgyud): b+hai ra be hUM huM/ oM badz+ra a mi ta hUM baM/ oM badz+ra ma ra ni hUM ho// 'di ni sh+tsar du pu ba shud kyi mgo can/ lhor bya rog gi mgo can/ nub dri srin bya'i mgo can no// byang du khri'i mgro
4b5(rgyud): can no// 'khor ba'i phur bu bsgrub don du/ 1dbang dang byin brlabs zhu ba'i phyir// ye shes khro bo gshegs su gsol// ye shes khro bo gshegs nas kyang // rtags dang ma
4b6(rgyud): ma bstan pa dang / phur pa'i dngos grub rtsal du gsol// dam tshig chen po'i dus la bab// sprul pa chen po'i dus la bab// pho nya chen po'i dus la bab// bdag nyid chen po'i dus
4b7(rgyud): lwa babya// sa bdag chen po'i dus la bab// khyi'i gdong can dus la bab// bsgral bar bya ba'i dus la bab// byang chub tu ni sems bskyed na sa// dus gsum sangs rgyas sras
5a1(rgyud): / bzhin du// rigs 'dzin bdag cag rnams la gzigs// gnod cing gdug pa'i dgra dang bgegs// bdud dang bar du gcod pa rnams// khro bo chen po'i
5a2(rgyud): byin brlabs kyis// yud tsam gyis ni de bkug nas// mngon spyod tshul gyis bsgral ba dang // lus ngag phye mar mdzad nas kyang // sdug bsngal nyams su myong bar mdzod// oM lam
5a3(rgyud): hUM lam stam b+ha naM/ mo hA ga tA u b+ha ga ban/ shrI kr-i bri kri badz+ra hUM ki ra hUM/ badz+ra ki li ki la ya dza hUM baM ho// sarba big nan/ badz+ra kI li kI la ya hU~M phaT// bgegs byed pa'i bdud rnams
5a4(rgyud): dang // sdug bsngal sems la mnyam spor ba// che ge mo zhes bya ba'i bdad// zungs shig gdungs shig rnam par chings// gtogs shig grogs dang dbye bar gyis// ring nas khug la
5a5(rgyud): smA ru chug pho ba cig rnam par gzir bar gyis// bdag gis dbang du byas gyur nas// bsgo ba'i bAka' nyan gus par gyis// hUM ma ra bid+yA ts+tshin+da ts+tshin+da hUM phaT/ bin+na bin+da hUM phaT/ g+hI na g+ha/ 
5a6(rgyud): d+hU phaTaN+Da ban+da ban+d+ha d+hu phaT/ tA sha ya t+yA shwA ya hU~M phaT/ trA sa ya ra da hr-i daN+Da hU~M phaH/ shi g+h+raM A na ya hU~M phaT/ dz+wa lA pa ya dz+wa la pa ya hUM/ a b+hi sha ya A b+hai sha ya hU~M phaT/ b+hin+da ya b+h+ya
5a7(rgyud): ya hUM phaT/ rje pho nya bran dang mngag pa'i tshogs// khyed kyi thugs dam dus la bag/ mngon spyod ji ltar nges pa dang // mngon spyod byin brlabs de bzhin mdzod// ta na ha na badz+ra/ dag
5b1(rgyud): badz+dza pA tsaM bats+ra b+haSh+TaM ma tha ma b+ha badz+ra/ dz+wa la dzA lar+b+hu badz+dzaHsu ru su ru badz+ra/ mu ru mu ruHbadz+dzad+hAka tr-i ka Ta yai/ dza ye bi dza yaHA dz+r-i te a pa ra dzi te/ mA ra sAM n+ya pra ma rbA ni hUM phaT/ rdo rje gsang ba
5b2(rgyud): bka' lung gis// sdug can gang zhig 'di'i byed pa// stobs chen khro bo chen po yas// mgo bo tshal pa brgya ru gyis// nyon cig bgegs dang lo ga 'dren rnams// nga'i bka'
5b3(rgyud): las 'da' ma byed// hUM ma ma bA shing ku ru// gdug cing sdang ba'i sems ldan rnams// slong shig lha min lha yang rung // nga la bar chad byed pa'i bdud// mthu dang rdzu 'phrul med par
5b4(rgyud): mdzod// sarba a na ya hUM phaT/ ta thA ya ta thA yA hUM phaT/ brdungs shig rdo rje 'bar ba'i gtun// bkra' las 'da' byed sdig tsan rnams// rdo rje me yi sti bsregs nasa?/ lus sems
5b5(rgyud): rdul bzhin brlag par mdzad// khro mo 'bar ba'i rdun khung du// rdo rje tho bas brdung byas nas// lha yang rung ste bsgral bar bya// kha taM kha taM/ kha taM hUM hUM hUM/ phaT phaT phaT/ badz+ra ye kA kro d+ha
5b6(rgyud): kha khA hi ha ha ha hUM hUM phaT phaT/ chos nyid kyi bden pa'o// gsang sngags kyi byin gyis brlabs so// sangs rgyas kyi byin kyi brlabs kyis mthur 'gyuraro// brnag pa de kho na nyid do// krI la ya/ lan
5b7(rgyud): nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlaso// kI la yaM bco brgyad brjod nas snying dkar nag gi mtsham su'o// hU~M hUM hUM/ ho ho ho/ phaT phaT phaT/ 'di brjod par bya'o// / rdo rje phur pa rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi dum bu/ slob
5b8(rgyud): dpon pad ma 'byung gnas/ dngos kyi rgyad pa dang mthun par/ dpal ldan sa skye paN+Di tas/ g.yas ru'i sa'i cha shangs kyi sreg shing du sbyar cing zhus te/ gtan la phab pa'o// 
6a1(rgyud): rgya gAr skad du/ shI bar+d+ha mAN+Da ai l-i kA ra na mA ma hA tA nA trai rA bod skad du/ dpa la rdo rje snying po rgyun ces bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyu la po chen po/ bla ma
6a2(rgyud): dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi zhabs kyi pad ma la spyi bor gus par phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa
6a3(rgyud): thams cad kyi rdo rje dang / nor bu da rin po tsho dang / pad ma dang / las kyis byin gyis brlabyas pa'i dam rlig gis ye shes rnam pa sna tshogs shing khyad par 'phags pa dang ldan pa/ 
6a4(rgyud): de bzhin ga/ shegs pa thams cad kyi ra na po che 'gacod pa na/ khams ka su mapa' sa kya ha lA por dbang bskaR+sha bya brnyas pa/ da bzhan gshAgs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje dam tshig gi
6a5(rgyud): ye shes rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgya brnyes pa/ de bzhin pa/ sheg pa thad kyi phyag rgya thad mo nyam pa nyid thugs su chud cing /  las
6a6(rgyud): / snga cho ga ste mdzad pa ma lus shing / lus pa med pa'i sems can gyi khAm+basmai thams ca'iSh+T+rIHhU~Mpa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa'i rdo rje'i lus mdzad pa/  thugs rje chen po rnam par snang
6a7(rgyud): mdzad chen po rtag pa/ dus gsum du gnas pa'i sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje de bzhin kau shegs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bsten cing bsngags pa'i nor
6a8(rgyud): bu rin po che chen po dang ldan pa/ khwa dog rnam pa sna tshogs pa'i gli lA bu btags pa/ rlung gis bskyod pa'i dAr gyi ba dan dang / me tog gi chun po dang /  bang+ga dA nga phyed pas
6b1(rgyud): klags shing nye bar mdzes pa/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad legs par yongs su dag pa chos kyi dbyings kyi khang bzangs dang / 'od mtha' yas pa/  shes rab kyi pha rol du
6b2(rgyud): byin pa'i gtsug lag khang / me tog gi khri shing mchog gi snying po'i rgyan gyis bkod pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud rgya mtshe rab tu bkram pa'i sprin/ nam mkha'i khams yongs
6b3(rgyud): su khyab pa de bzhin gshegs pas byin gyis brlabs pa/ mtha' las 'das pa'i sangs rgyas bkrung bya'i dbus/ rnam par snang mdzad kyi snying po// 'od gsal ba'i gzhal med khang/ 
6b4(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa'i gnas/ rdo rje snying po'i rgyan/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pa mi 'khrud mi 'gog par 'gog par mi
6b5(rgyud): 'gyur ba'i yan lag gi spyod yul yang dag pa'i mtha' gsal ba/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi yul/ chos kyi dbyings kyi snying po'i khang bzangs/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams
6b6(rgyud): cad kyi ye shes kyi sku/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub kyi snying pos chen po'i dam pa la bzhugs so// de la sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul dang mnyam pa'i
6b7(rgyud): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis yongs su bskul zhing mdun du bdur te chos ston par mdzad pa ni thog mar dge ba lnga du dge ba tha mA dag
6b8(rgyud): don bzang po// tshig 'bru bzang po ma 'dres pa/ yongs su rdzogs pa/ yongs su dag pa/ yongs su dkar gyi/ chos thams cad kyi tshul yongs su dag pa'i sgo ston par mdzad do// de nas
7a1(rgyud): yang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje gnyis su med pa mnyam pa nyid kyis ye shes dpa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
7a2(rgyud): / rnam par rgyal ba'i das rgyas gi 'thung gas so zhing sa thams can pa ny-id kyis nam dag pa'i tshe shem mnam pamamaman #
7a3(rgyud): tshogs pa'i phyag rgya'i ye shes thob pa/ sku dang gsung thugs rdo rje nam mkha' lta bu sku chen po rdo rje'i sku/ mtha' las 'das pa'i sku/ sku rin po che/ chos kyi sku/ sprul pa'i sku/ chos mnyam pa nyid
7a4(rgyud): kyi sku/ byang chub kyi sems don yod pa/ yongs su bsdus pa/ dge ba 'phel bya/  rgyal po snang ba'i tog/ bzhad pa po// chos dang ldan pa/ shes rab kyi 'khor lo// skad tham snga ma sna mas pa lu
7a5(rgyud): po gnod sprin can/ yang dag pa'i gter/ gtsug tor du gyur pa/ mchog ldan/ rdo rje can/ 'khor lo can/ ye shes can/  khyab bdag chen po// skra dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje/ nam mkha'i
7a6(rgyud): dbyings thams cad lta legs par bzhugs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis yongs su bgrod pas/ rdo rje'i dbyings thams cad khong du chud pa'i ye shes sems dpa'/ nam
7a7(rgyud): mkha'i khams thams cad kyi rdul phra rab kyi rdul dang mnyam pa'i rdo rje'i byin brlabs kyis ye shes snying po// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje rin po che'i dbang bskur ba chen po'i dam
7a8(rgyud): tshig/ nam mkha'i khams thams cad du spros pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mngon par shes pa mngon par byang chub par gyur pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag nyid kyi ngo bo
7b1(rgyud): rnam paR+Sha dag paste// chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin gyis dag pa/ namra mkha'o thams cad la khyab pa'o// gzugs thams cad yongs su mthong ba'i ye shes kyis ma lus shing lus pa
7b2(rgyud): med pa'i sems can 'dul ba'i spyod pa mchog dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad don yod pa'i bka' lung mdzad pas sems can mnyam pa nyid bla na med pa'i las sna tshogs pa
7b3(rgyud): can/ rnam snang mi 'gyur mi skyod pa/ b+h+rUM/ rin chen tog ste 'od byed pa// 'od dpag med pa rgyal ba'i mgon// don yod pas ni las kun byed/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi me long
7b4(rgyud): lta bu'i ye shes kyi dkyil 'khorade bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid kyi shes rab la rab tu gnas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi so sor rtog pa'i yed shes
7b5(rgyud): gnyis su med pa brnyes pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bya ba grub pa'i ye shes yang dag par rjes su thob pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag
7b6(rgyud): pa/ chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes kyi spyod yul/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gnyis su med cing mnyam pa nyid dmigs pa'i ye shes yongs su dag pa la gnas pa
7b7(rgyud): stong pa nyid dang de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i mtha' dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa dang / tshangs pa'i gnas bzhi po dag gis sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi yul du gyur pa/ sangs
7b8(rgyud): sa kyi yul mnyam po nyid la dmi gso ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rdo rje rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po nyid la byin gyis brlabs pa/ phyogs dang mtshams rnams la gnas pa
8a1(rgyud): rdo rje rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug gis 'jam dpal bzhon nur gyur pa la bka' stsal pa/ 'jam dpal khyod kyis sangs rgyas thams cad dang / rdo rje 'dzin pa rnams spyan
8a2(rgyud): drongs shig/ bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / 'jam dpal gzhon nur 'khor lo bsgyur ba chen po rab tu dgos pa'i zhal ras kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams
8a3(rgyud): cad dang rdo rje 'dzin pa rnams spyan drang ba'i don du rdo rje se gol gdabs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'das pa chen po'i snying po 'di ched du brjod pa/ bu d+hA sa ma dza aHha/ oM
8a4(rgyud): hUM badz+ra sa ma ya de nas de skad ces brjod pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang rdo rje 'dzin pa rnams kyis 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud rgya mtsho sprin khyab par mthong ngo // de nas
8a5(rgyud): yang 'jam dpal gzhon nur gyur pas// bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mjed dang / nade bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang gcig tu mdzad nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams
8a6(rgyud): cad kyi rdo rje blo gros kyi ye shes yongs su bskyed de rnam par gnas so// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzod de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i rang bzhin rnal 'byor gyi dang
8a7(rgyud): phyug gis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad du bdag nyid byin gyis brlabs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa de rnams dang rdo rje 'dzin pa rnams la bka' stsal pa/ kye de bzhin gshegs pa thams
8a8(rgyud): cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes 'khor lo bsgyur ba'i snying po bdag la/ yod de ngas bshad par bya yis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byin gyis rlobs shig/ b+h+rUM/ de nas mi skyod de bzhin
8b1(rgyud): ga shigs pA dang / s+yA rin chen 'byung gnas de bzhin gshegs// de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag myed/ don yod grub pa de bzhin gshegs// gzhan yang de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang lhan cig

8b3(rgyud): bzhir gyur te/ zhal bzhi po rnams las chos kyi dbyings dang nam mkha'i khams mtha' med pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul chos kyi tshul dbyangs gcig gis ched du brjod pa 'di lta ste/ rab tu dag
8b4(rgyud): pa rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de ni 'di ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// lta ba rnam par dag pa'i gnas g+ha yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so//  dga'
8b5(rgyud): ba rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// sred pa rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// 'dod tshogs rnam
8b6(rgyud): par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// zhe sdangapa rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so/ gti muge rnam par da
8b7(rgyud): pA'i gnas gang yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas s+ho/ nga rgyal rnam par dag pa'i gnas glang yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// mi khro ba rnam par dag pa'i
8b8(rgyud): gnas gang yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// yid che pa rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang 'ayin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// snang ba rnam par dag pa'i gnas ga/ 
9a1(rgyud): yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// lus rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// ngag rnam par dag pa'i gnas pa/ 
9a2(rgyud): yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// yid rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de na 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' gnas so// gzugs rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin/ 
9a3(rgyud): pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// sgra rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpe'i gnas so// dri rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de ni// 
9a4(rgyud): 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// ro rnam par dag pa'i gnas grong yin pa de ni 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa'i gnas so// reg rnam par dag pa'i gnas gang yin pa de ni la

9a6(rgyud): cang ni rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa ste/ chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pas shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa yongs su dag pa'o// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka
9a7(rgyud): stsal pa dang / chos thams cad kyi dbang phyug gsang bsngags thams cad kyi 'dren pa'o// bsngags thams cad kyi bla mar gyur pa'o// thams cad gtsug tor 'khor lo sgyur ba/ bstan pa la
9a8(rgyud): / rdzi ba med pa/ 'khor lo sgyur ba'i snying pos bka' stsal pa/ b+h+rUM/ 'jam dpal gang la las chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i snying po 'di lan cig tsam yang thos
9b1(rgyud): nas de'i byang chub kyi snying po la thug gI bar du nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / lus kyi sgrib pa thams cad kyis/ dmyal ba la sogs par skye bar myi 'gyur ro// gzhan yang sdig pa rnams sdug
9b2(rgyud): bsngal med cing zad par 'gyur ro// gang gis 'di 'chang ba dang nyi ma re rer 'don pa dang / ston pa dang / rgyun ma chad par yid la byed pa de ni skye bo 'di nyid la chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid
9b3(rgyud): rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin so sor thob nas chos thams cad kyi dbang phyug du 'gyur ro// chos thams cad la dga' zhing mgu la rab tu dga' ba myong bar 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa' chen po skye
9b4(rgyud): bya bcu drug na de bzhin gshegs pa nyid dam/ rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid thob par 'gyur ro// / hUM/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad kyis slar yang shes rab kyi pha
9b5(rgyud): rol du phyin pa'i tshul/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi zhi ba'i chos nyid mngon par byang chub pa'i rang bzhin 'di ston par mdzad do// rdo rje mnyam pa nyid mngon par byang chub pa'i byang chub
9b6(rgyud): chen po rdo rje lta bur sra bas/ don cig pa nyid kyis don mnyam pa nyid kyis don mnyam pa nyid mngon par byang chub pa'i byang chub chen po dang / rang bzhin rnam par dag pas chos mnyam pa
9b7(rgyud): nyid mngon par byang chub pa'i byang chub chen po dang / rnam par rtog pa dang / rnam pa mi rtog pas las thams cad mnyam pa nyid mngon par byang chub pas byang chub chen po ste/ 'jam dpal
9b8(rgyud): glang la las chos kyis gnas bzhi po 'di thob nas 'dzin pa dang / 'don pa pa dang / bsgom par byed na ji srid byang chub snying po la thug gi bar du/ sdig pa thams cad dang yang dag par ldan
10a1(rgyud): / pa yang sdig pa thams cad las grol bar 'gyur zhing myur du bla na med pa \u0f7f\u0f7fdA dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par byang chub par 'gyur ro// / oM/ de nas yang bcom ldan 'das
10a2(rgyud): gdug pa thams cad 'dul ba de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas chos thams can mnyam pa nyid rnam par rgyal ba bsdus pa zhes bya ba shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa nges par 'phrog pa bka' stsal
10a3(rgyud): pa/ 'dod chags kyi spros pa med pa'i phyir/ 'dod chags spros pa med pa'o// zhe sdang gi spros pa med pa'i phyir/ zhe sdang spros pa med pa'o// gti mug gi spros pa med pa'i phyir/ gti

10a7(rgyud): chos nyid brnyes pa'i de bzhin gshegs pas slar yang chos thams cad rnam par lta ba'i dbang phyug ye shes kyi phyag rgya zhes bya ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di bka' stsal pa/ 'jig
10a8(rgyud): rten gyi 'dod chags thams cad rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ yul thams cad rnam par dag pa nyid yin no// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rnam par dag pa'i phyir sdig pa thams cad rnam par

10b2(rgyud): chung mkhyen pa'i ye shes rnam par dag pa nyid yin no// 'jig rten gyi shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa rnam par dag pa'i phyir/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa rnam par dag pa nyid yin no// 
10b3(rgyud): 'jam dpal gang la las shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa 'di thos nas 'dzin cing 'don la bsgom par byed na de 'dod pa thams cad kyi nang nas gnas kyang pad ma lta bur 'dod chags kyi skyon blo bur ba'i

10b6(rgyud): byin pas 'jig rten gsum po thams cad kyi rgyal po yongs su thob par 'gyur ro// don gyi sbyin pas thams cad kyi bsam pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ro// chos kyi sbyin pas chos

10b8(rgyud): pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgya brnyes pa ni bzhin ga shegs pa thams cad kyi khu tshur 'chang de bzhin gsheg pa rtag pa slar yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes bya
11a1(rgyud): rgya byin gyis brlabs pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul bka' stsal pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku'i phyag rgya yongs su bzung bas/

12b1(rgyud): gnas gyur pa/ de srid mnyam med sems can don/ mya ngan mi 'da' byed par nus/ shes rab pha rol phyin pa'i thabs/ ye shes byin gyis brlabs kyis grug/ las ni thams cad rnam dag

13a1(rgyud): thams cad mnyam pa nyid la rab tu gnas pa'i de bzhin gshegs pas slar yang chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi mchog ces bya ba'i shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di bka' stsa la
13a2(rgyud): pa/ thams cad mnyam pa nyid pas shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa mnyam pa nyid dang / thams cad kyi don nyid pas shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i don nyid dang / chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid pas shes rab

14a1(rgyud): gyis bris pa dang / klag pa dang / brjod pa dang // rim gror bya ba dang / bla mar bya ba dang / rjed par bya ba dang / mchod par bya bar yang nus pa ma yin no// gang gis shes rab kyi pha

14a3(rgyud): can gang lha la gang gu'i klung gi bye ma brgyad bcu rnyed kyi sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig la phyag byas/ bla mar byas rjed par byas mchod par byas na/ des shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa'i tshul 'di nyan par

14b1(rgyud): kyimachog tu gas pe chen po mchog tu gsang ba'i dam tshig/ rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang phyug dam pa 'khor lo sgyur ba chen po bzhis yongs su bskor ba rdo rje snying po rgyan ces bya ba'i snying po 'di phyung ngo // mtshan
14b2(rgyud): nyid cig pa'i phyir chos thams cad gdod ma nas ma skyes pa'o// nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i phyir chos thams cad stong pa nyid do// spros pa thams cad spangs pa'i phyir chos thams cad gdod ma nas

15a1(rgyud): @snying pa'i rgyan byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ chos kyi dbyings kyi rdo rje chen po snying po'i rgyan de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i

20b5(rgyud): gA ti mug gi mtha' zhi ba'i phyir/ shes rab sgron ma rdo rje'i mtha' ste/ rdo rje'i mtha' 'dis mun pa sel bar byed par 'gyur ro// raM/ sems can thams cad sems gcig ste/

21a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas kyi chos te/ rdo rje'i mtha' 'dis thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rjes su rtogs pa las 'jug pa'i don dngardo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin rjes su rtogs pa'i

21a3(rgyud): su 'das pa'i don du 'gyur ro// hUMts+tsha// dag thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung ste/ rdo rje'i gnas 'dri sgra ji bzhin pa thams cad rjes su rtogs pa las 'jug pa'i don dang /

21a7(rgyud): 'gyur// de la sogs pa'i dngos grub thams cad dang // phun sum tshogs pa thams cad dran/ gter thams cad dang / 'khor lo thams cad dang / rdo rje thams cad dang / ral gri dang /

21b8(rgyud): rgyal po thob 'gyur na/ dngos grub gzhan lta ci zhig smos// gdugs dkar gtsug tor chen po ni// dam pa'i don du bsgom par bya// gtsug tor ye shes thob 'gyur na/ dngos grub
22a1(rgyud): / gzhan lta ci zhig smos// rgyal ba'i gtsug tor phyag rgya che// de ni yang dang yang du bsgom// chos kyi rgyal po rnam rgyal nyid// mdor bsdus pas ni thob par 'gyur//

22a5(rgyud): thob par 'gyur// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gtsug tor gyi dam tshig ye shes kyi phyag rgya rnams so// dra ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi yi ge'i rang bzhin gyi ye shes de la/ 
22a6(rgyud): bslab par bya'o zhes bya ba ni rnam par dpyod pa'i phyir chos thams cad kyi sgor shes par bya'o// a zhes bya ba ni chos thams cad ma skyes pa'i phyir chos thams cad kyi sgor bshad do// oM a AM aH/

22a8(rgyud): yongs su shes pa'i dbang du 'gyur ba'i phyir chos thams cad kyi sgor b+ha shad do// oM naM/ da zhes bya ba ni 'dul ba dang zhi ba'i pha rol du phyin pa yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i phyir chos thams
22b1(rgyud): cad kyi sgor brjod do// oM daM/ sa zhes bya ba ni yongs su nyon mongs pa dang / rnam pArA spong ba dang / zag pa dang bcas pa dang / zag pa med pa'i sgo nas phung po dang / khams dang skye mched la sog

23a1(rgyud): cad sgor blta bar bya'o// oM k+ShaM/ nga zhes bya ba ni chos thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi'ang yul ma yin pa'i phyir chos thams cad kyi sgor blta bar bya'o// aM daM/

24a1(rgyud): pa'i phyir chos thams cad kyi sgor blta bar bya'o// oM yA ra la wa/ mya ngan las 'das pa ni blo bur ba thams cad nges pa dor ba'i mtshan nyid dang / chos kyi

25a1(rgyud): ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas pan// rdo rje sems dpa' sems dpa' che/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshungs pa'i 'od// gtsug tor lnga ldan stobs po

25b4(rgyud): ngag ni de yis 'chad// chos kyi phyag rgya'i ye shes so// rdo rje las kyi phyag rgya che// dam pa'i don du bsgoms na ni// kun la kun nas rang nyid kyis// rdo rje las ni byed par 'gyur//

25b6(rgyud): stobs po che// dam pa'i don gyis bsgom par bya// rdo rje gnod sbyin dang mtshungs 'gyur// rdo rje dbyug gu'i phyag rgya che// lus ngag yid kyis de bzhin du// rdo rje'i sbyor bas bsgoms
25b7(rgyud): na ni// rdo rje khu tshur 'dzin par 'gyur// las kyi phyag rgya'i ye shes so// sgeg mos mngon par dga' ba ster// phreng ba yang na dbang bskur ba// glu mos mdzes pa'i sgra dbyangs byed/ 
25b8(rgyud): gar mas rdzu 'phrul thob par 'gyur// dri ma bzang po'i dri yin te// me tog byang chub yan lag nyid// sgron mas mtha' dag gsalta ba'o// 'dug pas bdug pa dag dang ldan// 
26a1(rgyud): / lcags kyus dbang phyug 'gugs byed na// skye bo gzhan dag smos ci dgos// zhags pas dang po'ang 'ching 'gyur na// bdug pas sems can smos ci dgos// 
26a2(rgyud): lcags sgrog gis ni 'phrog byed dang // tshangs sogs dbang phyug chen po'ang 'ching // 'bebs pas thams cad 'bebs 'gyur na// dman pa'i mi dag smos ci dgos// 'di nyid kyi ni sbyor
26a3(rgyud): bA yis/ ka chos kyi yi ge dang ldan pa'i// phyag rgya'i ye shes dang bcas pas// de dag thams cad myur du 'grub// 'di'i sbyor ba shes par bya// phyag rgya'i 'khor lo khyad par du// 
26a4(rgyud): spyi gtsug nas ni rkang pa'i bar// yi ge yis ni yongs gang bar// gzugs brnyan gcig ni go 'phang gyur// sems ni rtse gcig go 'phang gyur// sems ni rtse gcig 'gyur bar bsam/ 
26a5(rgyud): sa la rab gnas pad me ni// dbang chen gyi ni gnas zhes bshad// dbang po gnyis ni mya tshungs sbyor bas// dbang phyug kyang ni bsgrub par bya// dbang chen dag ni gru bzhi pa/ dbang
26a6(rgyud): chen gyi ni las su bshad// chu ni zlum por shes par bya// pad ma'i 'dab mas rnam par mtshan/ zhi bar byed pa'i las dang ldan/ zhi ba'i don du de bshad do// me ni gru gA sum shes
26a7(rgyud): par bya// bzhi mdo yi ni gnas su ba shang // dbang du bya ba bsgrub don du// pang mA rA gI 'dra ba'i 'od/ mngon spyod la ni brtson 'grus che// rlung gi dkyil 'khor dam pa ste// ral
26a8(rgyud): gri yi ni phyag rgya'i dbyings// dbyar gyi sprin dang mtshungs pa'i 'odi// srer dang da// rA dang de bzhin dmar// nag po yang ni khyad par du/ grwa dang po'i dkyil 'khor nas sbyar te// 
26b1(rgyud): mra'i bar du rab tu brtag/ dang por rdo rje rab tu gzhag/ de'i rjes su rin chen te/ pad ma dang ni las rnal 'byor// grub pa'i go 'phang rim par bshad// phyag rgya thams cad kyi ye shes so// 
26b2(rgyud): de nas bcom ldan 'das rtag pas de bzhin ga phyogs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya'i ye shes bka' stsal po/ gnyis su med pa yongs su dag pas chos thams cad rnam par grol ba'i phyag rgyas
26b3(rgyud): btab pa'o// / rtag pa dang chad pa yongs su dag pas/ chos thams cad zhi ba dang mtha' med pa'i phyag rgyas btab pa'o// / dang po zad pa dang bar du zad pa dang / tha mar zad pa dang ldan pas/ 
26b4(rgyud): chos thams cad zad pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mnyam pa nyid kyi mtha' rnam par dag pas chos thams cad la skur pa mi 'debs pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mig lnga la yang
26b5(rgyud): dag par 'das pas chos thams cad ni nam mkha'i phyag rgya rgyu btab pa'o// nam mkha'i khams thams cad dang ldan pas/ chos thams cad nam mkha'i rang bzhin gyis phyag rgyas rgyas
26b6(rgyud): btab pa'o// chos kyi dbyings yongs su khyab pas chos thams cad dbyer mi phyed pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// chos thams cad byang chub kyi sems dang tha mi dad pas/ chos tha
26b7(rgyud): cang byang chub kyi sems kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// chos kyi dbyings mi phyed pa'i mtshan nyid yin pas/ chos thams cad chos kyi dbyings kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// ngo bo nyid
26b8(rgyud): med pas chos thams cad stong pa nyid kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// 'tshe ba med pas chos thams cad bdag med pa'i phyag rgyas btab pa'o// ska cig ma nyid pas chos thams cid mi
27a1(rgyud): rtag pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// skye ba dang rga ba dang 'chi ba'i mtha' dang ldan pas/ chos thams cad sdug bsngal gyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// sngon gyi
27a2(rgyud): mtha' dang phyi ma'i de bzhin nyid pas chos thams cad de bzhin nyid kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// gdod ma nas yongs su dag pas/ chos thams cad yang dag pa'i mtha'i phyag rgyas rgyas
27a3(rgyud): btab pa'o// 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas mnyam pa nyid pas chos thams cad chen po steng pa nyid kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// spros pa'i dmigs pa rnam par bral bas chos thams cad
27a4(rgyud): mtshan ma med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// re ba thams cad las rnam byar grol bas chos thams cad smon pa med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyud
27a5(rgyud): kyis mtshan nyid kyis na/ chos thams cad mi rtag pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// phung po lnga yongs su 'dus pa'i mtshan nyid gyis ni chos thams cad sdug bsngal gyi phyag rgya rgyas btab
27a6(rgyud): pa'o// rang bzhin gyis bdag med pas chos thams cad med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// shin du mi g.yo ba'i phyir chos thams cad zhi ba'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// don dam
27a7(rgyud): pa'i bden pas yongs su khyab pa'i phyir chos thams cad bden pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// 'tsho ba rnam par mi gnas pa'i phyir chos thams cad dri ma med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// / 
27a8(rgyud): shin du gdon mi za bar gnas pa'i phyir/ chos thams cad 'khrul pa med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// sngon gyi mtha' dang phyi ma'i mtha' bcad pa'i phyir chos thams cad ji lta
27b1(rgyud): bya bzhin gyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mi rnams kyi gzhi med pa'i phyir chos thams cad kyi sgro 'dogs pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// byed pa pos byas pa'i phyir chos thams cad
27b2(rgyud): 'jig pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o//  rang bzhin gyis ma byung ba'i phyir chos thams cad 'byung ba med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o//  rang bzhin gyis ma skyes pa'i phyir chos thams cad
27b3(rgyud): 'gog pa med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// 'gag pa med pa'i phyir chos thams cad gdod ma nas skye ba med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// rnam par spyod pa kun du spyod pa thams
27b4(rgyud): nad dang bral ba'i phyir chos thams cad spros pa med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// gzugs rnam par blta ba med pa'i phyir chos thams cad mtshan nyid med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyaste btab
27b5(rgyud): pra'o// gnas yongs su bcad pa'i phyir chos thams cad nye bar sbyor ba med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mi mthun pa'i phyogs nye bar ma dmigs pa'i phyir chos thams cad skor pa mi
27b6(rgyud): 'debs pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mngon par 'du byed pa thams cad med pa'i phyir chos thams cad las kyi rnam par smin pa med pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// skye ba dang gnas
27b7(rgyud): pa las rnam par grol ba'i phyir chos thams cad 'dus ma byas pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// nam mkha' dang khyad par med pa'i phyir chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi phyag rgyas rgyas
27b8(rgyud): btab pa'o// mtshan nyid gcig pa'i phyir chos thams cad gzugs dang tshor ba dang 'du shes dang 'du byed dang / rnam par shes pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// nyon mongs pa
28a1(rgyud): med pa'i phyir chos thams cad phung po'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// nyon mongs pa dang banas pa med pa'i phyim chos thams cad khams dang skye mched kyi byas
28a2(rgyud): rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku dong mnyam pa nyid thob pas chos thams cad khams dang skye mched kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// mtha' gcig tu 'jog
28a3(rgyud): rten gyi lam rnam par dag pa'i phyir chos thams cad 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// lha'i rjes su byed pa'i phyir chos thams cad phyag rgya chen po'i phyag rgyas
28a4(rgyud): rgyas btab pa'o// mtha' gcig tu chos la phan 'dogs pa'i phyir chos thams cad chos kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// thams cad kyi las sna tshogs byed pa'i phyir chos thams cad
28a5(rgyud): lus kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// thams cad dam tshig thams cad rjes su bsgrub pa'i phyir chos thams cad dam rlig gi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams
28a6(rgyud): cang rab tu mi gnas pa'i phyir chos thams cad sangs rgyas kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// chos thams cad 'jig rte rje las 'das pa'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / theg pa chen po'i phyag rgya
28a7(rgyud): chu btab pa dang / gsang sngags kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / phyag rgya'i phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / dkyil 'khor gyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab dang / mnyam b+ha ny+tsi
28a8(rgyud): kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab po dang / rdo d+ha y-i shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btag pa dang / oM shes thams cad kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / mas cad man bya'o/ ya shes kyi bya
28b1(rgyud): rgyus rgyas btab pa dang / me long lta bu'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dngathams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / me long lta bu'i ye she
28b2(rgyud): kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / so sor rtog pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / bya ba grub pa'i ye shes
28b3(rgyud): kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa dang / chos thams cad chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyas rgyas btab pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes kyi phyag
28b4(rgyud): rgya'o// mu/ 'jam dpal phyag rgya'i tshig 'di dag ni mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i ye shes kyi tshigade bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i tshig/ thams cad
28b5(rgyud): mkhyen pa'i ye shes yongs su rdzogs par byed pa theg pa chen po'i tshig/ sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi phyag rgya'i tshig 'di rnams la/ 'das pa dang ma 'ongs po dang da ltar byung
28b6(rgyud): bla'i bcom ldan 'das rnams dang chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong dang / byang chub kyang byung ba yin no// a aM aHoM// sngags pas phyag rgya 'dis rgyas btab na/ de bzhin
28b7(rgyud): gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgyu dang ldan pa'i hUM myur du ma skyes pa'i chos rnams la bzod pa thob par 'gyur ro// de nas de ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sbyor ba thams cad
28b8(rgyud): kyi gsang ba chen po'i phyag rgya'i ye shes su gyur nasnying gi dbus su rtag tu bsgomasazla ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus son pam/ 'dab ma'i phreng zas 'phrogs pa'i 'od
29a1(rgyud): pad ma chen po 'dab brgyad pa// 'bar ba'i phreng bas 'khrigs pa'i 'od// de'i steng du rtag bsgom pa/ yi ge yi ni gtso bo mchog/ thog ma tha ma med zhi
29a2(rgyud): kha ba ba la dza 'o 'dra 'od/ dpa' bo kun 'da' zla ltar dka/ nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ltar 'od gsal/ zhi ba'i chos kyi rang bzhin sku// kun mkhyen ye shes kyis gang ba/ 
29a3(rgyud): de bzhin gshegs pa gnas kyi gsang // ra sa ya na dang mtshungs mchogakhaM yika mkha' 'drar shes ma pa bya// thig lai nA dAs rnam par smras// gsang ba chen po mchog
29a4(rgyud): gyi mdzesathog ma tha ma med pa'i bdag/ de'isteng du rdo rje che// rtse mo lnga dang yang dag ldan/ de'i steng du sgrol ma che/ 'byur ba'i phreng bas 'khrugs pa'i 'od// de'i
29a5(rgyud): steng du rtag bsam pa// yi ge mchog gi go 'bang ngo // man ngag mchog las shes bya ste/ gzhan du na ni nga mi smra// sangs rgyas mkhas pa thams cad kyis/ mdor bsdus
29a6(rgyud): nas ni 'di gsungs so// rnam par grol ba gsum thob nas// thob 'gyur 'di ni gzhan du mIn// l+ya ni rkon+do la sbyar bar bya// sna'i rtse mor yi ge hUM/ dbang po gnyis ni
29a7(rgyud): snyoms 'jug pas// phyag rgya'i go 'phang tshig gis ni// shes rab ldan pas rang sems bsgom// snang ba med cing spros med pa/ shin du mchog tu phrar shes bya// khyab
29a8(rgyud): bdug bsod nam sa ye shes dngos// bsam bya bsam gnas gcig byas te/ mr-ig dang skyon ma'i 'od bzhin du/ kun du 'bar ba dang ldan pa// mgrin pas 'bad pas btsum
29b1(rgyud): na sa ni/ dAkAr pr-i ser po sngon po'i 'od/ dmar po yang ni thams cad du// 'bar bya 'di dag 'bad pa yis/ sgrub po dam pas mtshon par bya/ snying khar gsal bar byas nas su//

29b3(rgyud): du// slar yang de ru 'ongs nas ni// de ni 'jug par rab tu bsam/ yid kyis de ltar bsgoms na ni/ rang nyid 'khor lo sgyur lta bus// dbang po lngas ni dmigs na ya / mi

29b5(rgyud): yongs bsten na// sngags pas mchog gi dngos grub thob// gsung sngags mchog tu dgyes pa na/ shes rab pha rol phyin pa che// zhi bu'i chos kyi rim pa ni// shin du mnyam par
29b6(rgyud): gzhag pa bsgom/ rdo rje sems dpa'i dngos grub gang // de 'grub gzhan lta smos ci dgos// mchog ni rtag par shes par bya// bar mas phun sum 'tshogs pa ste/ stong pa nyid dang
29b7(rgyud): mtshan med mchogasmon pa med pa zhes ni grags// chos kun bdag med pa'i mchog/ kun mkhyen ye shes rdzogs par byed// sa bcu yi ni stobs dag gis// pha rol phyin
29b8(rgyud): pa thams cad thob// rdo rje sems dpa' mchog bsgoms na/ rdo rje sems dpa' 'dra bar 'gyur/ de nyid 'di ni bcud kyis len/ gnyis su med pa'i ye shes mchog/ thegs
30a1(rgyud): /  chen mchog tu yid 'ong ba// stong nyid bsgom pa'i bdag nyid can// gnyis su med pa'i ye shes mchog/ gang gis rtag tu bsgom byed na// de'ang rdo rje 'dzin rgyal po// 
30a2(rgyud): yon tan mchog las skyes par 'gyur// bud med gang zhig sngo sangs ma// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam par brgyan// lus ngag yid kyi sbyor ba yis// yongs reg I la ngag tsum pas// 
30a3(rgyud): de tshe de ni bsngags pas bstan// mnyam med gsang ba'i ye shes mtshungs// bud med gang zhig kha dog dkar// pad ma'i mdab ma 'dra ba'o// de dang lhan cig bsngags pas bsdad// 
30a4(rgyud): dam pa'i dngos grub thob par 'gyur/ bu mo gang zhig kha dog dmar/ ud pa lo'i rgyan 'chang ma// bsngags pas de dang lhan cig gnas// shes rab pha rol phyin mtshungs
30a5(rgyud): 'gyur// bud med in dra ni la mtshungs// gsang ba rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gyis// bsngags pa chog shes pas bsten// rigs 'dzin rnams kyi stobs chen 'gyur// gsang chen
30a6(rgyud): mA ra ki ta mtshungs/ gang gis rtag tu bsten pa ni// de'ang rdo rje 'dzin rgyal po// myur du gsang ba'i dam par 'gyur// bud med pad mar gu 'dra// rgyan rnams kun gyis rnam
30a7(rgyud): par brgyan// dbang po gnyis ni snyoms 'jug pas// rdo rje 'dzin ma lta bu bsgrub/ sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam sbyor ba/ gnyis su med pa'i ye shes mchog/ gang gis
30a8(rgyud): rtag tu bsgom pa ni// mnyam med sangs rgyas kun dang mtshungs// dran pa nye bar gzhag pa bzhi/ mchog gi gnas gyis bsgoms na ni// rnal 'byor mchog gis mi ring bra
30b1(rgyud): rdo rje 'dzin pa lta bur 'gyur/ yang dgu spyod pa rnam pa bzhi/ legs par mnyam par gzhag pas bsgom/ dbang gnyis ni snyoms 'jug pas/ mnyam med 'jig rten dbang phyug
30b2(rgyud): mtshungs// skyo so yang dag rig pa bzhi/ shin du mnyam gzhag bsgoms na ni// zhen meng rdo rje sangs rgyas mtshungs// mnyam med 'jam pa'i mchog dang 'dra// mi 'jigs
30b3(rgyud): pa ni rnam pa bzhi/ rdo rje'i sbyor bas bsgom par bya// dbang po gnyis ni snyoms 'jug pas// rdo rje 'dzin pa lta bu ste// rdzu 'phrul gyi ni rkang pa bzhi/ shin du mnyam gzhag
30b4(rgyud): bsgoms na ni/ dbang po gnyis ni mnyam sbyor bas/ rdzu 'phrul ldan pa'i mchog tu 'gyur// tshangs pa yi ni gnas bzhi po/ tshad med pa'i sems kyi ni// rdo rje sbyor bar
30b5(rgyud): bdag bsgoms na// rdo rje 'dzin pa lta bu 'gru'o//  sbyor ba'i bdag nyid dbang po lnga// dam pa'i don gyis bsgoms na ni// dbang po gnyis ni snyoms 'jug pas// mnyam med
30b6(rgyud): rdo rje sangs rgyas mtshungs// yid kyi stobs ni rnam pa lnga// shin du mnyam gzhag bsgoms na ni// 'khor lo sgyur ba brtson 'grus che// stobs 'dzin lta bu nyid du 'gyur// byang
30b7(rgyud): chub yan lag rin chen bdun// gsang sngags bsgom pas bsgoms na ni// rtog pa'i ye shes sbyor ba'i// khyab bdag chos kun 'dzin par 'gyur// 'phags pa'i yan lag
30b8(rgyud): brgyad kyi lam/ kun mkhyen ye shes rdzogs byed pa/ de nas bsgoms pa tsam gyis ni// 'jig rten shes lus rab du 'dur// rjes su dran pa rnam pa drugabadag
31a1(rgyud): rtse gcig gis bsgoms na/ sngags pa rdo rje 'dzin pa ru sngag pa dus mi ring bar 'gyur// stobs bcu po ni yang dag bsgoms// bsgoms pa'i rnal
31a2(rgyud): 'byor de nyid kyis// bsod nams ye shes yongs rdzogs te// rtag tu stobs bcu'i dam par 'gyur// pha rol phyin bcu yongs su rdzogs// stobs rnams dang ni dbang rnams dang // 
31a3(rgyud): sa rnams kun ni nges bskyed nas// myur du mtshan ma dag par 'gyur// bud med nu ma shin du bsnun/ rje ngur rje dar de bzhin du// mchu yis mchu ni yongs su bzung // 'das pas
31a4(rgyud): dam du a ling ga/ rnam grol gos kyis bsgribs nas ni/ byang chub sems ni bsgom par bya// rdo rje ye shes brtson 'grus che// rdo rje dbyings su bdag brtan pas// rnam
31a5(rgyud): ba sna tshogs kang rA na// rnal 'byor shes pa des bsten bya// sngar bzhin thams cad byas nas su// bud med rnams kyi nyer gnas bsnun// sbyor ba 'di ni mkhyen pa yis/ 
31a6(rgyud): stobs chen sangs rgyas rab rgyu 'grub// gsang ba 'di ni dam pa ste// sangs rgyas kun gyis skyob pa'o// gsang ba 'di'i sbyor ba yi sku/ yi ge dam pa 'grub par 'gyur// 
31a7(rgyud): ma 'dres pa'i chos bco brgyadado// sangs rgyas chos su grags pa ste/ de rnams bsgom pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas byang chub rab ster byed// bsam gtan bzhi po thob
31a8(rgyud): nas ni// gzugs med pa'i rtag par yang // 'gog pa'i snyoms par 'jug ldan pas/ sangs rgyas byang chub bsgrub pa po/ byang chub phyogs ni sum bcu bdun/ 
31b1(rgyud): chos ni mchog tu rmed byung ba/ de rnams bsgom pa dang ldan pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i skyob pa'o// sngags rnams thams cad rab 'grub cing/ sbyor ba thams cad thams
31b2(rgyud): cad du'o// / des na 'bad pa thams nAd kyis// / sangs rgyasna chos nyid bsgom par bya// 'jig rten 'jig rten 'das pa'i lam/ ye shes rin chen rab rnyed dka'// mchod dang
31b3(rgyud): dbang bskur byin brlabs las/ rnyed 'gyur gzhan du ma yin no// zhu zhing ga stsol ba gdab pa dang // bdag nyid dbul ba de bzhin no// sangs rgyas sogs la yi rang zhing // 
31b4(rgyud): de bzhin yongs su bsngo ba dang // byang chub sems ni yang dag bskyed// khyad par du ni dus kun du'o// thog ma bar dang bye ma rnyed du/ ji lta bzhin du rjes bsgoms pas// sangs
31b5(rgyud): rgyas thams cad bsgrub bya ste// 'di la the tsom yod ma yin// 'gro ba sems kyis spro ba ni/ brtan pa'i snying por legs par bshadastong nyid de bzhin nyid las byung / 
31b6(rgyud): rdo rje sem sa dpa' de ba shad do/ d+ha\u0f88\u0f90 'gro ba thams cad bklag nas su// sangs rgyas byang chub spang bar bya// don yod ye shes dag pa de// rdo rje rgyal po mchog ces ba shadwa/ 
31b7(rgyud): rdo rje chags pas chags gyur nas/ rang bzhin gyis ni brtan par 'gyur/ 'gro ba ma lus lus med pa// de'i sems ni chags par bsha// chos rnams kun ni rang bzhin
31b8(rgyud): gyis// rnam par dben zhing gnyis su med// gang tshe dag pa'i bdag nyid mthong // de tshe rdo rje legs par bshad// rdo rje sems dpal bzhi po yi// ming dang badz+ra ni sbyor ba'o// 
32a1(rgyud): sangs rgyas kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// sdom pa mchog tu dam pa'o// khams gsum pa'i rgyal srid che// tshogs gnyis rdzogs par bya ste// sa dang
32a2(rgyud): pha rol phyin mchog rtse// rdo rje dbang bskur las byung ba// de bzhin gshegs kun ye shes te// rnyog pa med cing yi ge med// 'od kyi dkyil 'khor gzi brjid mchog/ brtan pa
32a3(rgyud): rtag pa nyid du gyur// nam mkha'i mdzod ni mdzod chen po// chos rnams thams cad legs gnas pa// yid bzhin nor bu rdo rje che// rdo rje tog ni bla na med// ye shes snang ba rin
32a4(rgyud): chen che// yongs su skye ba sogs su blta// de bzhin gshegs kun gasbyong ba ni// rdo rje bzhed pa zhes su bshad// chos kyi bdag med las byung ba// gnyis su med pa'i ye shes
32a5(rgyud): mchog/ chos nyid dam pa bas ma ru med// rdo rje chos zhes rab tu grugs// rdo rje blo gros snang ba che// shes rab ye shes dri med mchog/ zag med shes rab chen po pa// de ni rdo rje rno
32a6(rgyud): por bshad// sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos 'khor lo// gnyis su med las byung bar mtshon// yan lag bcu gnyis rten 'brel cing // rdo rje rgyu zhes nges par bshad// dgongs pa'i
32a7(rgyud): skad ni spros pa'i mchog/ yul rnams kyis ni bshad pa ste// sangs rgyas kun gyis bzlas pa che// de ni rdo rje smra bar bshad// sems can kun gyi don la sbyor// sangs rgyas kun gyi

44a8(rgyud): ni g.yo ba med pa ru// bdag nyid brtan par byas pa yis// mgon po chen po rnam snang mdzad// mi skyong rin tshon 'byung gnas dang // rgyal ba dag pa 'od dpag myed// don yod rgyal
44b1(rgyud): ba thams cad du/ rdul chu bcud len de nyid dang // mchog kyang rab tu gsol bar byed// dngos grub yid 'ong ma lus pa// rgyas pa'i don dang phun sum tshogs// re ba thams cad yongs rdzogs pa/

44b7(rgyud): sarba pran ti de sha yA mi swAhA// wA ka de'i rjes thogs la bdag nyid kyi dngos po dbul bar bya ste// // oM sarba ta thA ga ta nan Ad ma b+ha bi ni ra ya ta yA ma/ sarba te thA ga taHpra
44b8(rgyud): g+h+ri hA du maM swA hA// / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bsod nams la rjes su yi rang ba ni/ oM sarba ta thA ga ta pu n+ya dz+nyA na saM b+ha/ mAr na a nu mo da yA mi swAhA/ yang dang yang du bya
45a1(rgyud): / chub g+hi sems bskyed pa rang bzhin gyis grub pa'i sngags kyis bya ste// oM sarba ta thA ga ta sa man ta b+ha dA ma hA/ badz+ra sa ma yaM ma hA bo d+ha tsit+ta ud pa da yA mi swA hA// de nas
45a2(rgyud): byang chub kyi sems chen po bskyed pa'i rjes thogs la zla ba'i kha dog can zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la zhugs pa bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs pa sa bcu'i dbang phyug nor bu rin po che
45a3(rgyud): chen po'i pad ma'i snying po seng ge'i khri'i steng du bdag nyid bsam par bya'o// oM b+hu d+ho d+haM/ sngags 'dis bdag yongs su dag par bya ste/ oM sa b+hA bi shud+d+ha sarba ta thA ga ta/ sa b+ha ba shu d+ho taM/ 
45a4(rgyud): sngags 'dis bdag nyid chos kyi dbyings yangs pa 'od gsal ba'i snang bar shin du gnas par bya ste// // oM d+harma d+ha tu swa b+ha ba ud ma kro haM// de nas skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis
45a5(rgyud): kyis brgyan pa 'jig rten thams cad las shin du 'das pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi skur bdag nyid sngags 'dis gnas par bya ste// oM pra b+ha shA ro haM// de bzhin du ram pa 'dis

45a7(rgyud): yi ge la rjes su gzhol bar yid kyis 'bum phrag nyi shur bzlas par byas shing // nyi ma rI rer stong phrag brgyad dam stong phrag re bzlas te// ji srid mtshan ma thob pa de srid du'o// tsan dan dang / 
45a8(rgyud): ga pur dang / gur kum la sogs pa rnams kyis dkyil 'khor byas te/ nye bar mkho ba thams cad kyis mchod pa cho 'phrul gyi zla ba 'am sa ga'i nya gang pa la mar gyi mar me stong phrag brgyad spar la
45b1(rgyud): rdo rje dkyil dkrungs kyis gnas te/ sna ma'i me tog gram me rtog pad mas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / mchod rten mchod te ji srid 'brug gi sgra sgrogs pa ma thos de srid bzlas par bya'o/

46a1(rgyud): pa thams cad kyis mngon par gzigs par 'gyur ro// de'i rjes la lus dang ba gser gyi mdog lta bu dang lo brgyad gnyis kyi rnam pa can dang / ting nge 'dzin dang ye shes thob pa da
46a2(rgyud): khwa dog dang / tshe dang stobs dang shugs dang / dbang phyug la sogs pa'i yon tan dang ldan pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams rnams su rgyu ba dang / 'khor lo bsgyur ba ltar che ba dang / sangs rgyas thams
46a3(rgyud): cad kyis mngon par bstod cing steng du 'gro ba dang / rig pa 'dzin pa'i rgyal por 'gyur ba dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rig pa 'dzin pa brgya stong phrag du mas yongs

46b1(rgyud): bsgrub pa'i thabs zhes bya ba ste dang po'o// // bsgrub pa'i thabs gnyis pA ni de bzhin gA shegs pa thams cad mchod par byas te/ g+hi wang ngam ldong ros pad ma'i snod du gzhog la rdzi
46b2(rgyud): srid dngos grub rnam pa gsum byung ba de srid du bzlas par bya'o// sems can thams cad dbang du 'gyur ba dang / mi snang ba dang / rig pa thams cad 'dzin pa nyid do// rig pa 'dzin par gyur nas nyi ma

46b4(rgyud): su bskor ba dang / bskal pa chen po'i mthar gnas pa dang rig pa 'dzin pa thams cad kyi dbang phyug du 'gyur ro// rim pa 'dis rtse gsum bsgrubs na dbang phyug chen por 'gyur ro// s+ya mchod phyir

46b6(rgyud): dkyil 'khor byas te de'i steng du bsdad na/ nyi ma dang mtshungs par 'gyur ro// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyis zla ba steng 'di nyid kyis lha'i bye brag gang gis mtshan ma bzung ste/ des de'i long spong la

47a1(rgyud): brjod pas ltung ba dang / rgya mtsho skems pa dang /  ljon pa drung nas 'byin pa dang / bum pa nam mkha' la 'phen pa dang / glang po che rengs par byed pa dang / pha rol gyi
